<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports hierarchical data with unlimited depth levels</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Full keyboard navigation across all levels with arrow keys</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports single and multiple selections</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports both click and hover triggering modes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports looping keyboard navigation</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Built-in accessibility with ARIA roles and keyboard interactions</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports disabled items and read-only state</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Form integration with hidden input element</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports right-to-left direction</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the cascade select anatomy and part names.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="">No anatomy available for <!-- -->cascade-select</div>
<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the cascade select package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> cascadeSelect</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/cascade-select&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>These are the key exports:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code> - Creates a tree collection from your hierarchical data.</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="create-the-collection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Create the collection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#create-the-collection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code> function to create a tree collection from your hierarchical
data. Pass a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">rootNode</code> along with functions to extract each node&#x27;s value,
string label, and children.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> cascadeSelect <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/cascade-select&quot;</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">nodeToString</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>label<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">nodeToChildren</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span>children<span class="token punctuation">,</span>

<h3 id="create-the-cascade-select" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Create the cascade select<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#create-the-cascade-select"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Pass a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> so generated element ids stay predictable.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>

<h3 id="setting-the-initial-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initial value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initial-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> property to set the initial value of the cascade select.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>The <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> property must be an array of string paths. Each path is an array
of values from the root to the selected leaf item.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;north-america&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;us&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;ny&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> for controlled selection state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  value<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">setValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selecting-multiple-values" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selecting multiple values<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selecting-multiple-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To allow selecting multiple values, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code> property to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">multiple</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="hover-triggering" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Hover triggering<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#hover-triggering"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, items are highlighted when clicked. To highlight items on hover
instead (like a traditional cascading menu), set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightTrigger</code> property
to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;hover&quot;</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">highlightTrigger</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;hover&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="allowing-parent-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Allowing parent selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#allowing-parent-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, only leaf nodes (items without children) can be selected. To allow
parent (branch) nodes to also be selectable, set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">allowParentSelection</code> to
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">allowParentSelection</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="close-on-select" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Close on select<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#close-on-select"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the menu closes when you select an item. Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnSelect</code> to
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> to keep it open.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">closeOnSelect</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="looping-the-keyboard-navigation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Looping the keyboard navigation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#looping-the-keyboard-navigation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, arrow-key navigation stops at the first and last items. Set
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loopFocus: true</code> to loop back around.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">loopFocus</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>

<p>When an item is highlighted with the pointer or keyboard, use the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onHighlightChange</code> to listen for the change and do something with it.</p>

</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { highlightedValue: string[], highlightedItems: Item[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>

<h3 id="usage-within-a-form" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Usage within a form<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage-within-a-form"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To use cascade select in a form, pass <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code>. A hidden input is rendered with
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getHiddenInputProps()</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;location&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// In your JSX</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>input</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getHiddenInputProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>If the hidden input belongs to a different form element, also set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;location&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">form</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;checkout-form&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="validation-and-read-only-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Validation and read-only state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#validation-and-read-only-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">readOnly</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">required</code>, and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">invalid</code> to control interaction and form state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>cascadeSelect<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">readOnly</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">required</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">invalid</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each cascade select part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="open-and-closed-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Open and closed state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#open-and-closed-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the cascade select is open, the trigger and content is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code>
attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;open|closed&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for open or closed state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="selected-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selected state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selected-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Items are given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-state</code> attribute, indicating whether they are selected.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;checked|unchecked&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for selected or unselected state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="highlighted-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Highlighted state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#highlighted-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an item is highlighted, via keyboard navigation or pointer, it is given a
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-highlighted</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-highlighted</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for highlighted state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="branch-items" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Branch items<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#branch-items"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an item has children (is a branch node), it is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-has-children</code>
attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;item&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-has-children</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for items with children (branch nodes) */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Invalid state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the cascade select is invalid, the label and trigger is given a
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-invalid</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for invalid state */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the cascade select is disabled, the trigger and label is given a
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;label&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="empty-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Empty state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#empty-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The cascade select machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">TreeCollection&lt;T&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The tree collection data</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; label: string; control: string; trigger: string; indicator: string; clearTrigger: string; positioner: string; content: string; hiddenInput: string; list(valuePath: string): string; item(valuePath: string): string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the cascade-select elements. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name attribute of the underlying input element</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The form attribute of the underlying input element</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[][]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled value of the cascade-select</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[][]</code><span class="d_block">The initial value of the cascade-select when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the value.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled highlighted value of the cascade-select</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultHighlightedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial highlighted value of the cascade-select when rendered.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether to allow multiple selections</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">open</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The controlled open state of the cascade-select</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultOpen</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">The initial open state of the cascade-select when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the open state.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">highlightTrigger</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;click&quot; | &quot;hover&quot;</code><span class="d_block">What triggers highlighting of items</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">closeOnSelect</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the cascade-select should close when an item is selected</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loopFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the cascade-select should loop focus when navigating with keyboard</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em <h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/listbox" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">ListBox WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Space</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, opens the cascade select and focuses the first item.<br />When focus is on the content, selects the highlighted item.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Enter</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, opens the cascade select and focuses the first item.<br />When focus is on content, selects the highlighted item.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowDown</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, opens the cascade select.<br />When focus is on content, moves focus to the next item in the current level.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowUp</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on trigger, opens the cascade select and focuses the last item.<br />When focus is on content, moves focus to the previous item in the current level.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowRight</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on a branch item, expands the next level and moves focus into it.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowLeft</kbd></div><div><span>When focus is on a nested level, collapses it and moves focus back to the parent.<br />When focus is at the root level, closes the cascade select.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Home</kbd></div><div><span>Moves focus to the first item in the current level.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">End</kbd></div><div><span>Moves focus to the last item in the current level.</span></div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Esc</kbd></div><div><span>Closes the cascade select and moves focus to trigger.</span></div></li></ul><a cascade select component allows users to select from hierarchical data through\nmultiple linked levels of dropdown menus.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/cascade-select\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"CascadeSelect\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports hierarchical data with unlimited depth levels\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFull keyboard navigation across all levels with arrow keys\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports single and multiple selections\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports both click and hover triggering modes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports looping keyboard navigation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBuilt-in accessibility with ARIA roles and keyboard interactions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports disabled items and read-only state\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eForm integration with hidden input element\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports right-to-left direction\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the cascade select package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"cascade-select/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the cascade select anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"cascade-select\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the cascade select package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as cascadeSelect from \"@zag-js/cascade-select\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThese are the key exports:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ecollection\u003c/code\u003e - Creates a tree collection from your hierarchical data.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCreate the collection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003ecollection\u003c/code\u003e function to create a tree collection from your hierarchical\ndata. Pass a \u003ccode\u003erootNode\u003c/code\u003e along with functions to extract each node's value,\nstring label, and children.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003eimport * as cascadeSelect from \"@zag-js/cascade-select\"\n\ninterface Node {\n  label: string\n  value: string\n  children?: Node[]\n}\n\nconst collection = cascadeSelect.collection\u0026#x3C;Node\u003e({\n  nodeToValue: (node) =\u003e node.value,\n  nodeToString: (node) =\u003e node.label,\n  nodeToChildren: (node) =\u003e node.children,\n  rootNode: {\n    label: \"ROOT\",\n    value: \"ROOT\",\n    children: [\n      {\n        label: \"North America\",\n        value: \"north-america\",\n        children: [\n          {\n            label: \"United States\",\n            value: \"us\",\n            children: [\n              { label: \"New York\", value: \"ny\" },\n              { label: \"California\", value: \"ca\" },\n            ],\n          },\n          { label: \"Canada\", value: \"canada\" },\n        ],\n      },\n      {\n        label: \"Africa\",\n        value: \"africa\",\n        children: [\n          { label: \"Nigeria\", value: \"ng\" },\n          { label: \"Kenya\", value: \"ke\" },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCreate the cascade select\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e so generated element ids stay predictable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"cascade-select/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e property to set the initial value of the cascade select.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e property must be an array of string paths. Each path is an array\nof values from the root to the selected leaf item.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultValue: [[\"north-america\", \"us\", \"ny\"]],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled selection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e for controlled selection state.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSelecting multiple values\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo allow selecting multiple values, set the \u003ccode\u003emultiple\u003c/code\u003e property to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  multiple: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eHover triggering\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, items are highlighted when clicked. To highlight items on hover\ninstead (like a traditional cascading menu), set the \u003ccode\u003ehighlightTrigger\u003c/code\u003e property\nto \u003ccode\u003e\"hover\"\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  highlightTrigger: \"hover\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAllowing parent selection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, only leaf nodes (items without children) can be selected. To allow\nparent (branch) nodes to also be selectable, set \u003ccode\u003eallowParentSelection\u003c/code\u003e to\n\u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  allowParentSelection: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eClose on select\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the menu closes when you select an item. Set \u003ccode\u003ecloseOnSelect\u003c/code\u003e to\n\u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e to keep it open.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  closeOnSelect: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eLooping the keyboard navigation\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, arrow-key navigation stops at the first and last items. Set\n\u003ccode\u003eloopFocus: true\u003c/code\u003e to loop back around.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  loopFocus: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for highlight changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen an item is highlighted with the pointer or keyboard, use the\n\u003ccode\u003eonHighlightChange\u003c/code\u003e to listen for the change and do something with it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{3-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue: string[], highlightedItems: Item[] }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting the initial highlighted path\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003edefaultHighlightedValue\u003c/code\u003e to set the initially highlighted path.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultHighlightedValue: [\"north-america\", \u003ccode\u003eonHighlightChange\u003c/code\u003e to control highlighting\nexternally.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = property to listen for the\nchange and do something with it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4-7}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[][], items: Item[][] }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for open and close events\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eonOpenChange\u003c/code\u003e to listen for open and close events.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4-7}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean, value: string[][] }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlling open state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eopen\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonOpenChange\u003c/code\u003e for controlled open state, or },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCustom scroll behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003escrollToIndexFn\u003c/code\u003e to customize how each level scrolls highlighted items into\nview.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  formatValue(selectedItems) {\n    return selectedItems\n      .map((path) =\u003e path.map((item) =\u003e item.label).join(\" / \"))\n      .join(\", \")\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsage within a form\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo use cascade select in a form, pass \u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e. A hidden input is rendered with\n\u003ccode\u003egetHiddenInputProps()\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{4}\"\u003econst service = likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T2abc,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"A cascade select component allows users to select from hierarchical data through\nmultiple linked levels of dropdown menus.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/cascade-select\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"CascadeSelect\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Supports hierarchical data with unlimited depth levels\n- Full keyboard navigation across all levels with arrow keys\n- Supports single and multiple selections\n- Supports both click and hover triggering modes\n- Supports looping keyboard navigation\n- Built-in accessibility with ARIA roles and keyboard interactions\n- Supports disabled items and read-only state\n- Form integration with hidden input element\n- Supports right-to-left direction\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the cascade select package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"cascade-select/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the cascade select anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"cascade-select\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the cascade select package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as cascadeSelect from \"@zag-js/cascade-select\"\n```\n\nThese are the key exports:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n- `collection` - Creates a tree collection from your hierarchical data.\n\n### Create the collection\n\nUse the `collection` function to create a tree collection from your hierarchical\ndata. Pass a `rootNode` along with functions to extract each node's value,\nstring label, and children.\n\n```ts\nimport * as cascadeSelect from \"@zag-js/cascade-select\"\n\ninterface Node {\n  label: string\n  value: string\n  children?: Node[]\n}\n\nconst collection = cascadeSelect.collection\u003cNode\u003e({\n  nodeToValue: (node) =\u003e node.value,\n  nodeToString: (node) =\u003e node.label,\n  nodeToChildren: (node) =\u003e node.children,\n  rootNode: {\n    label: \"ROOT\",\n    value: \"ROOT\",\n    children: [\n      {\n        label: \"North America\",\n        value: \"north-america\",\n        children: [\n          {\n            label: \"United States\",\n            value: \"us\",\n            children: [\n              { label: \"New York\", value: \"ny\" },\n              { label: \"California\", value: \"ca\" },\n            ],\n          },\n          { label: \"Canada\", value: \"canada\" },\n        ],\n      },\n      {\n        label: \"Africa\",\n        value: \"africa\",\n        children: [\n          { label: \"Nigeria\", value: \"ng\" },\n          { label: \"Kenya\", value: \"ke\" },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Create the cascade select\n\n\u003e Pass a unique `id` to `useMachine` so generated element ids stay predictable.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"cascade-select/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initial value\n\nUse the `defaultValue` property to set the initial value of the cascade select.\n\n\u003e The `value` property must be an array of string paths. Each path is an array\n\u003e of values from the root to the selected leaf item.\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultValue: [[\"north-america\", \"us\", \"ny\"]],\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled selection\n\nUse `value` and `onValueChange` for controlled selection state.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  value,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    setValue(details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Selecting multiple values\n\nTo allow selecting multiple values, set the `multiple` property to `true`.\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  multiple: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Hover triggering\n\nBy default, items are highlighted when clicked. To highlight items on hover\ninstead (like a traditional cascading menu), set the `highlightTrigger` property\nto `\"hover\"`.\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  highlightTrigger: \"hover\",\n})\n```\n\n### Allowing parent selection\n\nBy default, only leaf nodes (items without children) can be selected. To allow\nparent (branch) nodes to also be selectable, set `allowParentSelection` to\n`true`.\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  allowParentSelection: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Close on select\n\nBy default, the menu closes when you select an item. Set `closeOnSelect` to\n`false` to keep it open.\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  closeOnSelect: false,\n})\n```\n\n### Looping the keyboard navigation\n\nBy default, arrow-key navigation stops at the first and last items. Set\n`loopFocus: true` to loop back around.\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  loopFocus: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for highlight changes\n\nWhen an item is highlighted with the pointer or keyboard, use the\n`onHighlightChange` to listen for the change and do something with it.\n\n```jsx {3-6}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { highlightedValue: string[], highlightedItems: Item[] }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Setting the initial highlighted path\n\nUse `defaultHighlightedValue` to set the initially highlighted path.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultHighlightedValue: [\"north-america\", \"us\"],\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled highlighted path\n\nUse `highlightedValue` and `onHighlightChange` to control highlighting\nexternally.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  highlightedValue,\n  onHighlightChange(details) {\n    setHighlightedValue(details.highlightedValue)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for selection changes\n\nWhen an item is selected, use the `onValueChange` property to listen for the\nchange and do something with it.\n\n```jsx {4-7}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[][], items: Item[][] }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for open and close events\n\nUse `onOpenChange` to listen for open and close events.\n\n```jsx {4-7}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  onOpenChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { open: boolean, value: string[][] }\n    console.log(details)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Controlling open state\n\nUse `open` and `onOpenChange` for controlled open state, or `defaultOpen` for an\nuncontrolled initial state.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  open,\n  onOpenChange({ open }) {\n    setOpen(open)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  defaultOpen: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Positioning submenu panels\n\nUse `positioning` to configure placement and collision behavior.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  positioning: {\n    placement: \"right-start\",\n    gutter: 4,\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Custom scroll behavior\n\nUse `scrollToIndexFn` to customize how each level scrolls highlighted items into\nview.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  scrollToIndexFn(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { index, depth, immediate? }\n    customScroll(details)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing the trigger label\n\nUse `formatValue` to control how selected paths are rendered in the trigger.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  formatValue(selectedItems) {\n    return selectedItems\n      .map((path) =\u003e path.map((item) =\u003e item.label).join(\" / \"))\n      .join(\", \")\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Usage within a form\n\nTo use cascade select in a form, pass `name`. A hidden input is rendered with\n`getHiddenInputProps()`.\n\n```jsx {4}\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  name: \"location\",\n})\n\n// In your JSX\n\u003cinput {...api.getHiddenInputProps()} /\u003e\n```\n\nIf the hidden input belongs to a different form element, also set `form`.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  name: \"location\",\n  form: \"checkout-form\",\n})\n```\n\n### Validation and read-only state\n\nUse `readOnly`, `required`, and `invalid` to control interaction and form state.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(cascadeSelect.machine, {\n  id: useId(),\n  collection,\n  readOnly: true,\n  required: true,\n  invalid: false,\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach cascade select part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Open and closed state\n\nWhen the cascade select is open, the trigger and content is given a `data-state`\nattribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"open|closed\"] {\n  /* styles for open or closed state */\n}\n```\n\n### Selected state\n\nItems are given a `data-state` attribute, indicating whether they are selected.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-state=\"checked|unchecked\"] {\n  /* styles for selected or unselected state */\n}\n```\n\n### Highlighted state\n\nWhen an item is highlighted, via keyboard navigation or pointer, it is given a\n`data-highlighted` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-highlighted] {\n  /* styles for highlighted state */\n}\n```\n\n### Branch items\n\nWhen an item has children (is a branch node), it is given a `data-has-children`\nattribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-has-children] {\n  /* styles for items with children (branch nodes) */\n}\n```\n\n### Invalid state\n\nWhen the cascade select is invalid, the label and trigger is given a\n`data-invalid` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for invalid state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for invalid state */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled state\n\nWhen the cascade select is disabled, the trigger and label is given a\n`data-disabled` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"label\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled label state */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"item\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for disabled item state */\n}\n```\n\n### Empty state\n\nWhen no option is selected, the trigger is given a `data-placeholder-shown`\nattribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-placeholder-shown] {\n  /* styles for empty state */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe cascade select machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"cascade-select\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe cascade select `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"cascade-select\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"cascade-select\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"cascade-select\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\nAdheres to the\n[ListBox WAI-ARIA design pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/listbox).\n\n### Keyboard
